\DoxyCodeLine{07506\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07507\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ is\ an\ implementation\ of\ wcwidth()\ and\ wcswidth()\ (defined\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07508\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ IEEE\ Std\ 1002.1-\/2001)\ for\ Unicode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07509\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07510\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ http://www.opengroup.org/onlinepubs/007904975/functions/wcwidth.html}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07511\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ http://www.opengroup.org/onlinepubs/007904975/functions/wcswidth.html}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07512\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07513\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ In\ fixed-\/width\ output\ devices,\ Latin\ characters\ all\ occupy\ a\ single}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07514\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ "{}cell"{}\ position\ of\ equal\ width,\ whereas\ ideographic\ CJK\ characters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07515\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ occupy\ two\ such\ cells.\ Interoperability\ between\ terminal-\/line}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07516\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ applications\ and\ (teletype-\/style)\ character\ terminals\ using\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07517\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ UTF-\/8\ encoding\ requires\ agreement\ on\ which\ character\ should\ advance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07518\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ cursor\ by\ how\ many\ cell\ positions.\ No\ established\ formal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07519\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ standards\ exist\ at\ present\ on\ which\ Unicode\ character\ shall\ occupy}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07520\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ how\ many\ cell\ positions\ on\ character\ terminals.\ These\ routines\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07521\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ a\ first\ attempt\ of\ defining\ such\ behavior\ based\ on\ simple\ rules}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07522\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ applied\ to\ data\ provided\ by\ the\ Unicode\ Consortium.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07523\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07524\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ For\ some\ graphical\ characters,\ the\ Unicode\ standard\ explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07525\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ defines\ a\ character-\/cell\ width\ via\ the\ definition\ of\ the\ East\ Asian}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07526\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ FullWidth\ (F),\ Wide\ (W),\ Half-\/width\ (H),\ and\ Narrow\ (Na)\ classes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07527\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ In\ all\ these\ cases,\ there\ is\ no\ ambiguity\ about\ which\ width\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07528\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ terminal\ shall\ use.\ For\ characters\ in\ the\ East\ Asian\ Ambiguous\ (A)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07529\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ class,\ the\ width\ choice\ depends\ purely\ on\ a\ preference\ of\ backward}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07530\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ compatibility\ with\ either\ historic\ CJK\ or\ Western\ practice.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07531\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Choosing\ single-\/width\ for\ these\ characters\ is\ easy\ to\ justify\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07532\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ appropriate\ long-\/term\ solution,\ as\ the\ CJK\ practice\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07533\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ displaying\ these\ characters\ as\ double-\/width\ comes\ from\ historic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07534\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ implementation\ simplicity\ (8-\/bit\ encoded\ characters\ were\ displayed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07535\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ single-\/width\ and\ 16-\/bit\ ones\ double-\/width,\ even\ for\ Greek,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07536\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Cyrillic,\ etc.)\ and\ not\ any\ typographic\ considerations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07537\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07538\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Much\ less\ clear\ is\ the\ choice\ of\ width\ for\ the\ Not\ East\ Asian}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07539\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ (Neutral)\ class.\ Existing\ practice\ does\ not\ dictate\ a\ width\ for\ any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07540\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ of\ these\ characters.\ It\ would\ nevertheless\ make\ sense}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07541\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ typographically\ to\ allocate\ two\ character\ cells\ to\ characters\ such}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07542\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ as\ for\ instance\ EM\ SPACE\ or\ VOLUME\ INTEGRAL,\ which\ cannot\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07543\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ represented\ adequately\ with\ a\ single-\/width\ glyph.\ The\ following}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07544\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ routines\ at\ present\ merely\ assign\ a\ single-\/cell\ width\ to\ all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{07545\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ neutral\ characters,\ in\ the\ interest\ of\ simplicity.\ This\ is\ not}}
